***впасть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a> (7546)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpastʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впадать.html>впада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(river)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to flow <i>(into)</i></li>
<li><i>(a condition)</i> to fall <i>(into)</i>, to lapse <i>(into)</i>, to sink <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:задумчивость.html>заду́мчивость</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v zadúmčivostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отчаяние.html>отча́яние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v otčájanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give way to despair; be driven into despair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сомнение.html>сомне́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v somnénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to begin to have doubts</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> неми́лость</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v nemílostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into disfavour/disgrace</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:детство.html>де́тство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v détstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enter one's second childhood; be in one's dotage</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впасть.html>впасть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чие</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpastʹ</b> v protivoréčije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">contradict oneself</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(cheeks, eyes etc.)</i> to sink in, to become hollow/sunken</li></ol>

</ul></li>

</ol>

***впечатление.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ние</a> (1102)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впечатли́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpečatlítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Eindruck</i>, which in turn is a calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">impression</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpečatlénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>impression
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатление.html>впечатле́ние</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:влюбиться.html>влюби́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>дру́га</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U menjá <b>vpečatlénije</b>, što oní vljubílisʹ v drug drúga.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm under the impression that they've fallen in love with each other.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатлять.html>впечатля́ть</a> (17340)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">впечатл-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpečatl-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to impress

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впечатляющий.html>впечатля́ющий</a> (14248)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатляющий.html>впечатля́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpečatljájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатлять.html>впечатля́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpečatljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впечатляющий.html>впечатля́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpečatljájuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>impressive</li></ol>

***впиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a> (13638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(into)</i>, to pierce, to bite <i>(into)</i>, to drive one's sting <i>(into)</i>, to dig one's fangs <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуба́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpivátʹsja</b> zubámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's teeth (into)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>когтя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpivátʹsja</b> kogtjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's claws (into)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fix one's eyes <i>(on)</i>, to fix with one's eyes, to fasten one's eyes <i>(upon)</i>, to glue one's eyes <i>(to)</i></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вписывать.html>впи́сывать</a> (24999)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписывать.html>впи́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpísyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписать.html>вписа́ть</a></b>)

<ol><li>to enter, to insert <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">something to the text that is already written by writing</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<li>to inscribe</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписывать.html>впи́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpísyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpísyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписаться.html>вписа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blend <i>(with)</i>, to fall in <i>(with)</i>, to fit <i>(into)</i></li>
<li>to fit <i>(into)</i>, to fit in <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́ши</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́ны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">éto ne <b>vpísyvajetsja</b> v náši plány</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it doesn't agree [fit in] with our plans</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписывать.html>впи́сывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpísyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:далее.html>Да́лее</a>, закупившись <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дкой</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пельмень.html>пельме́нями</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> какой-то <a href = vnd.unilang:живность.html>жи́вностью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>пошли́</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:вписываться.html>впи́сываться</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хата.html>ха́ту</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рама.html>Ра́ме</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>
<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>частичн.: дописываться, <a href = vnd.unilang:записываться.html>запи́сываться</a>, приписываться</li>
<li>частичн.: <a href = vnd.unilang:вмещаться.html>вмеща́ться</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:входить.html>входи́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:умещаться.html>умеща́ться</a></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впитывать.html>впи́тывать</a> (15015)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впитать.html>впита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vpitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впитывать.html>впи́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpítyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впитать.html>впита́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soak up, to soak in, to drink in, to absorb, to imbibe, to take in, to sop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впитывать.html>впи́тывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молоко.html>молоко́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpítyvatʹ</b> s molokóm máteri</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to imbibe with one's mother's milk/at one's mother's knees</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a> (8059)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vpítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впиваться.html>впива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stick <i>(into)</i>, to pierce, to bite <i>(into)</i>, to drive one's sting <i>(into)</i>, to dig one's fangs <i>(into)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:зуб.html>зуба́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpítʹsja</b> zubámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's teeth (into)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:коготь.html>когтя́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vpítʹsja</b> kogtjámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to dig one's claws (into)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fix one's eyes <i>(on)</i>, to fix with one's eyes, to fasten one's eyes <i>(upon)</i>, to glue one's eyes <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:впиться.html>впи́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>vpílsja</b> v nejó glazámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he couldn't take his eyes off her</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
